IMPFED_unit_naming = {
	no_dominion_namelists = {
		available = {
			has_completed_focus = ENG_imperial_federation
		}

		visible = {
			NOT = { has_country_flag = no_dominion_namelists }
		}

		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 0
		}
		complete_effect = {
			set_country_flag = no_dominion_namelists
		}
	}	
	no_imperial_namelists = {
		available = {
			has_completed_focus = ENG_imperial_federation
		}

		visible = {
			NOT = { has_country_flag = no_imperial_namelists }
		}

		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 0
		}
		complete_effect = {
			set_country_flag = no_imperial_namelists
		}
	}
}	

ENG_imperial_conference_decision = {
	
	IMPFED_imperial_conference_decision = {

		icon = generic_political_discourse
		
		available = {
			hidden_trigger = { always = no }
		}

		days_mission_timeout = 60

		fire_only_once = yes

		activation = {
			tag = ENG
			has_country_flag = IMPFED_imperial_conference_timer_flag
		}

		visible = {
			tag = ENG
			has_country_flag = IMPFED_imperial_conference_timer_flag
		}

		cancel_if_not_visible = no

		is_good = yes

		complete_effect = {
			
		}

		timeout_effect = {
			custom_effect_tooltip = imperial_conference_ends_tt
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						AND = {
							is_subject_of = ENG
							tag = CAN
						}
						AND = {
							is_subject_of = ENG
							tag = SAF
						}
						AND = {
							is_subject_of = ENG
							tag = RAJ
						}
						AND = {
							is_subject_of = ENG
							tag = AST
						}
						AND = {
							is_subject_of = ENG
							tag = NZL
						}
						AND = {
							has_country_flag = IRE_attended_conference
							tag = IRE
						}
					}
				}	
				#remove_opinion_modifier = { target = ENG modifier = ENG_imperial_conference_opinion }
				remove_opinion_modifier = { target = ENG modifier = ENG_imperial_conference_approved_resolution }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						IRE = {
							is_subject_of = ENG
						}
					}
				}	
				IRE = { add_opinion_modifier = { target = ENG modifier = ENG_attended_conference } }
				ENG = { add_opinion_modifier = { target = IRE modifier = ENG_attended_conference } }
			}
		}
	}
	
	ENG_invite_ireland_to_conference = {
		
		icon = generic_political_discourse
		
		allowed = {
			tag = ENG
		}
		available = {
			NOT = {
				has_country_flag = ENG_imperial_conference_discussion_in_progress
				IRE = { has_country_flag = invited_to_imperial_conference }
			}
			has_government = democratic
		}

		cost = 50
		
		fire_only_once = yes
		
		
		visible = {
			has_completed_focus = ENG_imperial_conference
			has_country_flag = IMPFED_imperial_conference_timer_flag
			country_exists = IRE
		}
		
		complete_effect = {
			country_event = { id = IMPFED_events.1 hours = 6 }
			set_country_flag = ENG_imperial_conference_discussion_in_progress
		}
	}

	IMPFED_discuss_imperial_federation = {

		icon = eng_imperial_federation

		allowed = {
			tag = ENG
		}

		available = {
			NOT = { has_country_flag = ENG_imperial_conference_discussion_in_progress }
			OR = {
				CAN = { exists = yes }
				SAF = { exists = yes }
				AST = { exists = yes }
				NZL = { exists = yes }
				AND = {
					RAJ = { is_subject_of = ENG }
					has_completed_focus = ENG_indian_autonomy
				}
			}
		}

		cost = 100

		fire_only_once = yes

		visible = {
			has_completed_focus = ENG_imperial_conference
			has_country_flag = IMPFED_imperial_conference_timer_flag
		}

		complete_effect = {
			country_event = { id = IMPFED_events.99 hours = 6 }
			set_country_flag = ENG_imperial_conference_discussion_in_progress
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { has_completed_focus = ENG_indian_autonomy }
				}
				custom_effect_tooltip = ENG_indian_autonomy_tt
			}
		}

		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 100
		}
	}
}
IMPFED_expand_the_federation = {  #EXPANDING THE FEDERATION - 10 PP per 250,000 pop, 10pp per 2 factory slots (base, no tech)
	integrate_ireland = {
		available = {
			113 = {
				is_owned_by = ROOT
				compliance > 50
			}	
			135 = {
				is_owned_by = ROOT
				compliance > 50
			}	
			134 = {
				is_owned_by = ROOT
				compliance > 50
			}	
			has_equipment = {
			    infantry_equipment > 2000
			}
			NOT = {
				country_exists = IRE
			}
		}
		visible = {
			113 = {
				is_owned_by = ROOT
				NOT = { is_core_of = ROOT }
			}	
			135 = {
				is_owned_by = ROOT
				NOT = { is_core_of = ROOT }
			}	
			134 = {
				is_owned_by = ROOT
				NOT = { is_core_of = ROOT }
			}
			NOT = {
				country_exists = IRE
			}
		}
		
		cost = 150
		
		fire_only_once = yes

		days_remove = 70
		
		modifier = {
			weekly_manpower = -300
			stability_weekly = -0.02
		}
		
		complete_effect = {
			add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
			    type = infantry_equipment
			    amount = -2000
			}
		}	
		
		remove_effect = {
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					is_core_of = IRE
				}
				add_core_of = ROOT
			}
			add_stability = 0.2
		}
	}

	development_in_the_uk = {
		available = {
			any_state = {
					OR = {
						region = 1
						region = 2
						region = 3
						region = 4
					}
				is_owned_by = ROOT
				is_controlled_by = ROOT
				is_core_of = ROOT
			}
			NOT = { has_country_flag = IMPFED_development_in_progress }
		}	
		
		visible = {
			any_state = {
					OR = {
						region = 1
						region = 2
						region = 3
						region = 4
					}
				is_owned_by = ROOT
			}
		}	
		
		cost = 70
		
		days_remove = 70
		
		complete_effect = {
			set_country_flag = IMPFED_development_in_progress
		}
		
		remove_effect = {
			random_state = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						region = 1
						region = 2
						region = 3
						region = 4
					}
					is_owned_by = ROOT
					is_controlled_by = ROOT
					is_core_of = ROOT
				}
				add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = 1
				random_list = {
					20 = {
						add_building_construction = {
							type = industrial_complex
							level = 1
							instant_build = yes
						}	
					}	
					20 = {
						add_building_construction = {
							type = arms_factory
							level = 1
							instant_build = yes
						}	
					}	
					20 = {
						add_building_construction = {
							type = dockyard
							level = 1
							instant_build = yes
						}
						modifier = {
							factor = 0
							is_coastal = no
						}
					}
					20 = {
						add_building_construction = {
							type = synthetic_refinery
							level = 1
							instant_build = yes
						}	
					}
					20 = {
						add_building_construction = {
							type = infrastructure
							level = 1
							instant_build = yes
						}	
						modifier = {
							factor = 0
							free_building_slots = {
								building = infrastructure
								size < 1
							}		
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

	FRA_integrate_algeria = {
		available = {
			tag = FRA
			459 = {
				is_owned_by = ROOT
				compliance > 50
			}
			460 = {
				is_owned_by = ROOT
				compliance > 50
			}
			513 = {
				is_owned_by = ROOT
				compliance > 50
			}
		}
		visible = {
			tag = FRA
			459 = {
				is_owned_by = ROOT
				NOT = { is_core_of = ROOT }
			}
			460 = {
				is_owned_by = ROOT
				NOT = { is_core_of = ROOT }
			}
			513 = {
				is_owned_by = ROOT
				NOT = { is_core_of = ROOT }
			}
		}
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 1
			modifier = { # to avoid nuking stability
				factor = 0
				has_stability < 0.3
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.5
				has_stability < 0.5
			}
			modifier = {  # to encourage law changes instead
				factor = 0
				has_manpower < 10000
			}	
			modifier = { # to encourage spending on advisors first
				factor = 0.5
				amount_taken_ideas = {
					amount > 3
					slots = {
						political_advisor
					}
				}
			}	
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.5
				amount_taken_ideas = {
					amount > 3
					slots = {
						high_command
					}
				}
			}	
			modifier = { # because this focus locks France out of their own coring focus
				factor = 2
				has_completed_focus = FRA_encourage_immigration
			}	
			modifier = { # because this is the end of the French integration tree
				factor = 0.5
				has_completed_focus = FRA_french_union
			}
		}
		
		cost = 280
		
		fire_only_once = yes

		days_remove = 70
		
		modifier = {
			stability_weekly = -0.02
		}
		
		complete_effect = {
			ENG = {
				country_event = {
					id = IMPFED_events.47
				}
			}
		}
		
		remove_effect = {
			459 = { add_core_of = ROOT }
			460 = { add_core_of = ROOT }
			513 = { add_core_of = ROOT }
			add_stability = 0.2
		}
	}

					}
				}
			}	
			modifier = { # to encourage POR to do their own thing instead
				factor = 0.5
				has_completed_focus = POR_luso_tropicalism
			}	
		}

			}	
			modifier = { # to encourage spending on advisors first
				factor = 0.5
				amount_taken_ideas = {
					amount > 3
					slots = {
						political_advisor
					}
				}
			}	
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.5
				amount_taken_ideas = {
					amount > 3
					slots = {
						high_command
					}
				}
			}	
		}
		complete_effect = {
			ENG = {
				country_event = {
					id = IMPFED_events.47
				}
			}
			add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
			    type = infantry_equipment
			    amount = -2000
			}
		}
		
		remove_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { 
					MEN = { is_subject_of = ROOT }
					MAN = { is_subject_of = ROOT }
				}
				annex_country = {
					target = MEN
					transfer_troops = yes
				}
				annex_country = {
					target = MAN
					transfer_troops = yes
				}
			}
			716 = { add_core_of = ROOT }
			328 = { add_core_of = ROOT }
			717 = { add_core_of = ROOT }
			714 = { add_core_of = ROOT }
			715 = { add_core_of = ROOT }
			610 = { add_core_of = ROOT }
			761 = { add_core_of = ROOT }
			611 = { add_core_of = ROOT }
			621 = { add_core_of = ROOT }
			add_stability = 0.2
		}
	}

IMPFED_world_revolution = {
	ally_supported_rebels = {
		available = {
			tag = ENG
		}
			
		visible = {
			any_other_country = {
				has_country_flag =  rebelled_with_IMPFED_help
			}	
		}
			
		target_trigger = {
			has_country_flag = rebelled_with_IMPFED_help
			is_subject = no
			is_in_faction = no
			NOT = { is_in_faction_with = ROOT }
		}
		
			
		complete_effect = {
			set_autonomy = {
				target = FROM
				autonomy_state = autonomy_puppet
			}	
		}
		
	}
	incite_revolution_in_libya = {
		available = {
			has_equipment = { infantry_equipment > 2499 }
			has_equipment = { support_equipment > 99 }
			has_equipment = { artillery_equipment > 124 }
		}
			
		visible = {
			NOT = {
				country_exists = LBA
				any_state = {
					is_core_of = LBA
					is_owned_by = ROOT
				}	
			}
		}
			
		days_remove = 90
			
		complete_effect = {
			add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
				type = infantry_equipment 
				amount = -2000
			}
			add_equipment_to_stockpile = {	
				type= support_equipment 
				amount = -100
			}
			add_equipment_to_stockpile = {	
				type = artillery_equipment 
				amount = -250
			}
		}
		remove_effect = {
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					is_core_of = LBA
					NOT = {
						OR = { 
							is_owned_by = ROOT
							owner = {
								is_subject_of = ROOT
							}
						}	
					}
				}	
				owner = {
					release = LBA
					declare_war_on = {
						target = LBA
						type = annex_everything
					}	
				}	
			}	
			LBA = {
			
				set_politics = {
					ruling_party = communism
				}
				set_popularities = {
					communism = 60
					democratic = 20
					fascism = 20
				}
				add_ai_strategy = {
					type = alliance
					id = ENG
					value = 1000
				}
				add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
					type = infantry_equipment 
					amount = 2000
				}
				add_equipment_to_stockpile = {	
					type= support_equipment 
					amount = 100
				}
				add_equipment_to_stockpile = {	
					type = artillery_equipment 
					amount = 250
				}
				country_event = {
					id = IMPFED_events.50
				}
			}
		}
	}

				country_exists = EQG
				any_state = {
					is_core_of = EQG
					is_owned_by = ROOT
				}	
			}
		}
			
		days_remove = 90
			
		complete_effect = {
			add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
				type = infantry_equipment 
				amount = -2000
			}
			add_equipment_to_stockpile = {	
				type= support_equipment 
				amount = -100
			}
			add_equipment_to_stockpile = {	
				type = artillery_equipment 
				amount = -250
			}
		}
		remove_effect = {
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					is_core_of = EQG
					NOT = {
						OR = { 
							is_owned_by = ROOT
							owner = {
								is_subject_of = ROOT
							}
						}	
					}
				}	
				owner = {
					release = EQG
					declare_war_on = {
						target = EQG
						type = annex_everything
					}	
				}	
			}	
			EQG = {
			
				set_politics = {
					ruling_party = communism
				}
				set_popularities = {
					communism = 60
					democratic = 20
					fascism = 20
				}
				add_ai_strategy = {
					type = alliance
					id = ENG
					value = 1000
				}
				add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
					type = infantry_equipment 
					amount = 2000
				}
				add_equipment_to_stockpile = {	
					type= support_equipment 
					amount = 100
				}
				add_equipment_to_stockpile = {	
					type = artillery_equipment 
					amount = 250
				}
				country_event = {

ENG_move_to_secure_the_dominions_neutrality = {
	
	ENG_impose_martial_law_on_canada_neutrality = {

		icon = generic_civil_support

		allowed = {
			tag = ENG
		}

		available = {
			NOT = { army_manpower_in_state = { state = 467 amount < 4500 } }
			NOT = { army_manpower_in_state = { state = 469 amount < 4500 } }
			NOT = { army_manpower_in_state = { state = 470 amount < 4500 } }
			NOT = { army_manpower_in_state = { state = 473 amount < 4500 } }
			NOT = { army_manpower_in_state = { state = 465 amount < 4500 } }
			NOT = { army_manpower_in_state = { state = 464 amount < 4500 } }
			NOT = { army_manpower_in_state = { state = 468 amount < 14400 } }
			NOT = { army_manpower_in_state = { state = 276 amount < 24000 } }
		}

		targets = { CAN }
		targets_dynamic = yes

		target_root_trigger = {
			has_completed_focus = ENG_a_change_in_course
			NOT = {
				OR = {
					has_completed_focus = ENG_organize_the_blackshirts
					has_completed_focus = ENG_concessions_to_the_trade_unions
				}
			}
		}

		target_trigger = {
			FROM = {
				original_tag = CAN
			}
		}

		cost = 50

		fire_only_once = yes

		days_remove = 180

		visible = {
			OR = {
				has_government = democratic
				has_government = neutrality
			}
			OR = {
				has_country_flag = ENG_abdication_crisis_morganatic_marriage
				has_country_flag = ENG_abdication_crisis_normal_marriage
				has_country_flag = edward_viii_married_wallis_simpson
			}	
			NOT = { 
				OR = {
					has_completed_focus = ENG_organize_the_blackshirts
					has_completed_focus = ENG_concessions_to_the_trade_unions
					has_country_flag = ENG_abdication_crisis_changed_mind
				}
			}	
			FROM = {
				is_subject_of = ROOT
				NOT = { has_country_flag = ENG_imperialist_civil_war }
				NOT = { has_country_flag = ENG_loyalty_enforced }
			}
		}

		cancel_if_not_visible = yes

		modifier = {
			political_power_factor = -0.1
		}

		remove_effect = {
		}

		complete_effect = {
			FROM = {
				hidden_effect = { set_country_flag = { flag = ENG_cannot_leave_faction value = 1 days = 180 } }
				custom_effect_tooltip = ENG_impose_martial_law_tt
				country_event = { id = mtg_britain.63 }
			}
			add_stability = -0.03
			add_war_support = -0.02
		}

		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 0
		}
	}

	ENG_propaganda_campaigns_in_canada_neutrality = {

		icon = eng_propaganda_campaigns

					}
				}
			}
			add_stability = -0.05
		}

		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 0
		}
	}

					has_completed_focus = ENG_organize_the_blackshirts

			}

					has_completed_focus = ENG_concessions_to_the_trade_unions

			if = {

					has_government = fascism

				NOT = { has_country_flag = ENG_imperialist_civil_war }
				NOT = { has_country_flag = ENG_loyalty_enforced }

			}
		}

			political_power_factor = -0.1
		}

		remove_effect = {
		}

		complete_effect = {
			FROM = {
				hidden_effect = { set_country_flag = { flag = ENG_cannot_leave_faction value = 1 days = 180 } }
				custom_effect_tooltip = ENG_impose_martial_law_tt
				country_event = { id = mtg_britain.63 }
			}
			add_stability = -0.05
			add_war_support = -0.02
		}

		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 0
		}
	}

IMFPED_commonwealth_research_decisions = {
	IMPFED_reform_commonwealth_research = {
		
		allowed = {
			tag = ENG
		}

		available = {
			OR = {
				CAN = { is_subject_of = ROOT }
				AST = { is_subject_of = ROOT }
				SAF = { is_subject_of = ROOT }
				NZL = { is_subject_of = ROOT }
				RAJ = { is_subject_of = ROOT }
			}
		}
		
		visible = {
			tag = ENG
			NOT = {
				is_in_tech_sharing_group = commonwealth_research
			}
		}

		fire_only_once = yes
		
		cost = 150
		
		complete_effect = {
			add_to_tech_sharing_group = commonwealth_research
			if = {
				limit = {
					CAN = {
						is_subject_of = ROOT
					}
				}
				CAN = { add_to_tech_sharing_group = commonwealth_research }
			}	
			if = {
				limit = {
					AST = {
						is_subject_of = ROOT
					}
				}
				AST = { add_to_tech_sharing_group = commonwealth_research }
			}	
			if = {
				limit = {
					NZL = {
						is_subject_of = ROOT
					}
				}
				NZL = { add_to_tech_sharing_group = commonwealth_research }
			}	
			if = {
				limit = {
					SAF = {
						is_subject_of = ROOT
					}
				}
				SAF = { add_to_tech_sharing_group = commonwealth_research }
			}	
			if = {
				limit = {
					RAJ = {
						is_subject_of = ROOT
					}
				}
				RAJ = { add_to_tech_sharing_group = commonwealth_research }
			}	
		}
	}	

	IMPFED_expand_commonwealth_resarch = {
		
		allowed = {
			tag = ENG
		}

		
		visible = {
			tag = ENG
			is_in_tech_sharing_group = commonwealth_research
		}

				has_country_flag = IMPFED_diplo_puppeted

		}
	}
